for name, symbol in SYMS.items():
    t = ticker(symbol)
    v = volume_profile(symbol)

    d = {
        **t,
        "funding_history_pct": funding(symbol),
        "oi_change_5m_pct": oi_change(symbol, "5min"),
        "oi_change_15m_pct": oi_change(symbol, "15min"),
        "oi_change_1h_pct": oi_change(symbol, "1h"),
        "oi_change_4h_pct": oi_change(symbol, "4h"),
        "orderbook_imbalance_pct": orderbook(symbol),
        **v,
    }

    d["market_state_flags"] = market_state(d, weekend_flag)
    spot[name] = d

out = {
    "ts_bucharest": now.strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S"),
    "weekend_flag": weekend_flag,
    "spot": spot,
    "global": global_data()
}

    oi = get_all_oi()
    ob = get_orderbook(limit=200)
    trades = get_recent_trades(limit=1000)
    vol = get_volume_structure()
    global_data = get_global()

    btc = {}
    btc.update(ticker)
    btc.update(funding)
    btc.update(oi)
    btc.update(ob)
    btc.update(trades)
    btc.update(vol)
    btc["market_state_flags"] = build_flags(btc)

    return {
        "ts_bucharest": now.strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S"),
        "weekend_flag": weekend_flag,
        "instrument": instrument,
        "btc": btc,
        "global": global_data
    }

if __name__ == "__main__":
    out = build_snapshot()
    print("===API_SNAPSHOT_START===")
    print(json.dumps(out, ensure_ascii=False))

def build():
    now = datetime.now(ZoneInfo("Europe/Bucharest"))
    out = {
        "ts_bucharest": now.strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S"),
        "weekend_flag": now.weekday() >= 5,
        "instrument": instrument_info(),
    }

    btc = {}
    btc.update(ticker("linear", SYMBOL_PERP))
    btc.update(funding_history())
    btc.update(all_oi())
    btc.update(orderbook("linear", SYMBOL_PERP, 200))
    btc.update(recent_trades("linear", SYMBOL_PERP, 1000))
    btc.update(volume_and_structure("linear", SYMBOL_PERP))
    btc.update(spot_perp_divergence())
    btc["market_state_flags"] = flags(btc)

    out["btc"] = btc
    out["global"] = global_data()
    return out

if __name__ == "__main__":
    snapshot = build()
    print("===API_SNAPSHOT_START===")
    print(json.dumps(snapshot, ensure_ascii=False))
    print("===API_SNAPSHOT_END===")
